General Assembly of Stranded Employees of the Shenyang Arsenal 112

Going to the Municipal Government Today to Petition

Requesting Measures to Maintain Livelihood

After the violent Japanese forcibly occupied Liaoning, more than 2,100 people who had escaped from the Shenyang Arsenal had come to Shanghai. For the sake of livelihood, a general meeting was held the day before yesterday to discuss measures, and it was decided to go to the municipal government today to petition. The details of the various situations are recorded below.

General Assembly At 9 AM on the morning of the day before yesterday, a general assembly of all stranded personnel was convened at the Qu Zhenren Temple, with more than 700 people attending. Dai Xiuqi was publicly elected as the chairman. First, the chairman reported on the experiences of being stranded and the purpose of the meeting, and then the discussion began. It was resolved: (1) Wang Wenlong, Dai Xiuqi, Lu Youke, Zhang Longshun, Zhu Qiming, Yu Guilin, and other six people were designated as responsible representatives of all stranded personnel. (2) It was decided to go to the municipal government to petition on the 12th. (3) Wang Yongtao and Wu Shunfu were designated as leaders during the petition. (4) Zhang Tai'an, Qu Jinshan, Xie Qingtian, Liu Caiqin, Chen Qikai, and Gu Changde were designated as inspectors during the petition.

Petition to the Municipal Government The stranded personnel of the Shenyang Arsenal decided to gather at the Qu Zhenren Temple at 8 AM this morning and go to the municipal government to petition at 10 AM. The text of the petition is recorded as follows: "We are submitting this petition because we were driven out by the violent Japanese and are displaced. We cry all the way and sincerely request relief to maintain our lives. Since the Japanese invaders used conspiracies and coercive means to invade and occupy Shenyang, slaughter our soldiers and civilians, occupy our factories, and seize our weapons, their various atrocities are too numerous to mention. All those with blood and qi feel heartbroken when they speak of it and gnash their teeth when they hear of it. Moreover, the representatives and other workers are employed in the provincial arsenal and have been personally harmed. They all want to eat the flesh and sleep on the skin of the Japanese and be satisfied. Now that the national crisis is imminent, we are not concerned about our family difficulties. We only think that the reason why our country is weak and despised by others is that although there are more than one reason, the most important reason is the lack of elite military strength. The representatives and others belong to the workers and should fulfill the obligations of the workers, but the Fengtian Arsenal has been lost and there is no way to serve the country. We can only call for nothing. Therefore, more than 2,000 people who have escaped to Shanghai have been living in thatched huts in places such as the Qu Zhenren Temple on Xiejiao Road, sleeping on the ground and having no rice to cook. The pain is indescribable. Yesterday, all the stranded employees were convened to hold a meeting and decided to first petition the government, requesting: (1) The stranded employees who have come to Shanghai are all from other provinces and are stranded in the middle of the road, suffering from cold and hunger. We request that food be distributed daily from now on to maintain the status quo and protect our lives. (2) The workers will go to Beijing to petition, requesting notification from the Jinghu Railway Bureau to issue free round-trip train tickets. (3) The workers have worked in the Feng factory for two and a half months and have not been paid. We request that the government forward a telegram to Deputy Commander Zhang to pay the arrears so that the family members can be safely sent back to their hometowns. (4) The workers originally belonged to the workers and have some experience in manufacturing weapons. We request that measures be taken to accommodate them to assist the country's work and fulfill their own livelihood. It is really convenient for both public morality. The matter is urgent. We crawl on the ground and wait for orders. We cannot bear to pray for the utmost."

The executive committee will convene shop employees and shop owners in Shanghai to discuss thorough measures; (9) To appoint Xiao Bichuan, Lin Youren, Zhang Chuming, Guo Zhenjia, Zeng Tianmin, Yang Qingxuan, and Guo Feilin to be responsible for drafting and publishing the association's telegrams, declarations, and other documents; (10) The executive committee will hold its first meeting on October 15, convened by the joint association of Fujianese organizations in Shanghai.

Zhabei Military Police Corps Joint Defense Meeting 117

The Infantry Second Regiment of the Ministry of Finance's Tax Police Corps, stationed in the Qianjiang Guild Hall on Taiyangmiao Road in Zhabei, which is responsible for guarding the Northern Shanghai District, convened its first joint defense meeting of military police corps yesterday. The meeting was attended by more than twenty people, including the regimental and battalion commanders of the Second Regiment, Gu Dinghua, Wu Guanzhou, Teng Tieshan, Li Weiping, Liu Tianshao, Song Zhuoyu, Li Tiezheng, Liu Dongxuan, Shen Yulin of the Second Battalion of the Military Police, Han Tiexian and Liu Guoshu of the Fourth and Fifth Police Districts, Wang Xisan of the police offices of the Beijing-Shanghai and Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo railways, and Bu Liheng and Li Xiuling of the Shanghai North Defense Corps. After the ceremonial procedures, Chairman Colonel Gu reported that his regiment was ordered to be responsible for security in the Northern Shanghai area, in accordance with Article 6 of the Shanghai Garrison Command's security plan, which stipulates that the security forces in each district should convene a defense meeting once a week with local military police agencies within their respective districts. Moreover, as his regiment had just arrived in this area, it was not familiar with the local situation, and at a time when the situation was turbulent, there were many things that needed to be discussed with everyone. Furthermore, with the Japanese invasion of our Northeast, all citizens are filled with righteous indignation, and the indignation of our armed comrades must be even deeper. They should be the vanguard of the people and annihilate these tyrannical elements. However, before receiving orders from the central government, we should do our best to avoid meaningless conflicts, which would disrupt the national plan. Recently, students from various schools in Shanghai and other places have organized propaganda teams to publicize everywhere in order to awaken compatriots and inspire popular morale, and they should be protected. He noted that there are many Japanese residents and soldiers in Shanghai, and conflicts may inevitably occur. The police should pay special attention to protecting Japanese residents properly before relations are severed in order to avoid complications. The current order in each district will be maintained by the police for the time being, and the troops will provide assistance at any time if needed. The discussion then proceeded as follows: (1) The Northern Shanghai District is vast, and the military police are scattered. How should they communicate? Resolution: Each agency will draw a rough map of the deployment locations of its forces and fill in telephone numbers, which will be sent to the regimental headquarters for compilation and distribution to the responsible officials for reference. At the same time, a request will be submitted to the Garrison Command, instructing the Zhabei Telephone Bureau to connect telephone lines to facilitate communication between them; (2) All units should still be on alert at all times and await orders; (3) How to clarify the situation in each location? Resolution: In addition to the regimental headquarters sending plainclothes detectives to conduct reconnaissance in different directions, each agency should promptly communicate with each other using the simplest methods if they hear anything; (4) Prohibit soldiers in uniform from entering the concession and arresting soldiers who are out without symbols to prevent trouble? Resolution: It is easiest to cause misunderstandings when soldiers in uniform enter the concession, and the police should dissuade them. If they do not listen, they can be detained and sent to the regimental headquarters for processing. If soldiers are seen without insignia, they should be immediately detained and sent to their respective agencies for strict handling; (5) Omitted; (6) How to devise simple communication methods for ordinary times for use in emergencies? Resolution: In the event of a major event requiring troop assistance and the telephone cannot be used, the facts can be recorded, omitting unnecessary details, and only the time, address, and event should be clearly stated and sent by letter to the nearest garrison in each district for immediate assistance.

Preliminary Meeting First

Decision Made to Issue Declaration Later

Regarding the convening of the Fourth Roundtable Conference of the Pacific International Association, the association's secretary, Mr. Loomis, told a reporter from the Xin Sheng News Agency yesterday afternoon that the conference was originally scheduled to open in Hangzhou on the 22nd of this month, but whether the conference can be held will depend on a preliminary meeting to be convened this Tuesday. It was resolved to hand it over to the Standing Committee for verification and issuance; (15) Should another declaration be issued regarding Japan's protest against the patriotic movement in our country? It was resolved to continue to issue a declaration, and Committee Member Tan Yigong was appointed on the spot to draft it; (16) Cases submitted by various specialized anti-Japanese committees: (A) Not cooperating with Japanese lawyers; (B) Immediately terminating cases that have been accepted by Japanese clients, and not allowing any to be accepted if they have not been accepted; (C) Not allowing to defend or handle negotiations for people who have been sanctioned by the anti-Japanese association; (D) Members who rent Japanese houses are requested to terminate the lease as soon as possible; (E) Announcing the Japanese atrocities and collecting members to give lectures; (F) Founding a publication; (G) Hosting lawyers from various countries. It was resolved to hand over the above cases to the Standing Committee for deliberation and handling; (17) Send a telegram to Geneva Minister Shi Zhaoji for discussion. It was resolved to appoint Committee Member Li Shirui to amend and send it; (18) Lawyers Shu Weiyuan, Wang Bangfan, Huang Zongzhou, Feng Xizui, Yao Qiyin, Du Yuesong, Ding Zheng, Zhang Zhenwan, and Chen Wen applied to join the association. It was resolved to pass the applications. After the discussion, the meeting adjourned.

Case of the Great China Rubber Factory 126

Anti-Japanese Conference Decides on Disposal Method

The factory has been ordered to resume work immediately.

Because the Great China Rubber Factory previously had a small amount of Japanese raw materials in stock (such as red lining cloth, which has now been abandoned), someone reported it to the Anti-Japanese National Salvation Association. It happened that the factory's manager, Nie Fuji, was representing the rubber industry trade association at the Domestic Goods Manufacturers' Congress. The Anti-Japanese Association ordered him to temporarily seal the small amount of old Japanese raw materials in stock. As previously reported, it is heard that the Anti-Japanese Association sent people to the factory to investigate and learned that the factory had been determined to improve its products since its opening to achieve the goal of completely domestic goods. However, in terms of raw materials, except for calcium carbonate, which is manufactured in a factory in Rihuigang and can be supplied, the rest are ordered from Western merchants and will be available in Shanghai soon. In order to protect domestic goods and the livelihoods of the factory workers, the Anti-Japanese National Salvation Association decided at its regular meeting to order the factory to resume work immediately to maintain the livelihoods of the workers. The factory's small amount of raw materials will be jointly re-examined and unsealed by the Inspection and Investigation Departments. After receiving the notice, the factory has already complied with it.

Oppose Changzhou Cocoon Business Tax 129

According to a report from its members, the Shanghai Silk Factory Trade Association stated that when purchasing autumn cocoons from Changzhou County, they were illegally extorted by business tax collectors, resulting in the seizure of boats. They telegraphed the National Government Finance Ministry, the Jiangsu Provincial Government, the Finance Department, and the Changzhou County Government yesterday, instructing them to investigate and handle the matter. The telegram stated that the Yigong Silk Factory reported that recently, when purchasing autumn cocoons from various villages in Changzhou County, Jiangsu Province, they were illegally extorted by local collectors of business taxes, resulting in boat seizures and fines. The business tax authority employs former liquor tax office staff who regard extorting merchant ships as their usual practice. In addition to harassing cocoon merchants, they have also established patrol boats at Henglin, Zhoutieqiao, Anqiao, and Jujiangqiao in the county to arbitrarily demand money from passing cocoon boats. Even cocoon boats purchased from Yixing County are not exempt. If they are slightly dissatisfied, they seize the boats and impose heavy fines. If the tax ticket is not carried on the boat or if the goods of one shipment are shipped in batches and the tax ticket cannot be prepared for each boat, then each boat is fined 30 yuan, 28 yuan, or 16 yuan. Even if a tax ticket is carried on the boat, a handling fee of 2 yuan must be paid per boat. Such open extortion is utterly unscrupulous and cannot be tolerated under the flag of honesty. It is requested to forward the matter to the government and order a stop to this and to investigate and severely punish the violators to demonstrate fairness and alleviate the merchants' difficulties. It was decided at the 12th temporary representative assembly on the 3rd of this month to submit the matter to request a thorough investigation. The practice of collecting liquor tax was the most notorious during the Qing Dynasty, and our government, regretting its harm to the country and its damage to merchants, followed the guidelines of the late Prime Minister and resolutely abolished it. It is unimaginable that the Changzhou County business tax office is now resuming its old tricks, and it is no wonder that merchants and people are heartbroken. According to the report, it is requested to order a stop to this and thoroughly investigate and handle the matter.

Record of the General Meeting of All Members of the Former French Concession Chinese Volunteer Corps 131

The Former French Concession Chinese Volunteer Corps held a general meeting of all members on the 6th of this month at No. 6, Belle Road, Tianxiang Men's Benevolent Hall. The officers present included Corps Commander Wang Shunfa, Machine Gun Squad Leader Wang Renrong, Squadron Leaders Chen Qingyu and Zhu Binlong, Military Medical Officer Chen Jiaren, Platoon Leaders Ke Enqing, Li Shengzu, Cao Qichao, Hu Yukang, Bao Dingyuan, Cai Jicai, Chu Qingxiang, Zhao Laiyuan, and more than 80 members. The meeting began at 7:00 PM. Corps Commander Wang Shunfa was elected as chairman and reported the purpose of the meeting, stating that the corps had been suspended for two years since Chief Commander Wei resigned because no one was in charge. The corps has a glorious history and is a group of citizens, and it is not appropriate to suspend it for a long time. Therefore, the meeting was convened for joint discussion. As a result of the meeting, a restoration committee was organized, named the French Concession Chinese Volunteer Corps Restoration Movement Association, to carry out all restoration matters and to send a letter to the French Concession Chinese Taxpayers Association and a document to the French Consul General, Mr. Grogelin, and the Police Chief, Mr. Favreau, requesting that people of integrity and prestige in the concession be appointed as soon as possible to restore the corps' duties immediately so that the spirit of the corps in the past can be maintained and the security of the concession can be greatly assisted. It happened to be raining heavily at the time of the meeting, and all the members came in the rain, which is truly admirable.

News of Disaster Relief 136

Relief Committee Denies Sale of American Wheat in Shanghai 137

To be transported to various disaster areas for distribution after arriving in Shanghai.

The National News Agency reports that local newspapers have previously reported that the first batch of American wheat would arrive in Shanghai, and the authorities were planning to sell the wheat on the market. The National Government's Water Disaster Relief Committee considers this unfounded rumor to be baseless and sufficient to disrupt the market. It is hereby denied. Regarding the use of American wheat, Article 7 of the contract (already seen in various newspapers) stipulates that it is exclusively for charitable relief in Chinese water disaster areas, with a clear meaning. It is reported that the first batch of 8,000 tons of relief wheat has been shipped from Seattle on the slave-operated Aola steamboat. It will be transported to various disaster areas for distribution after arriving in Shanghai at the end of this month to implement the policy of work relief.

Representatives from Northern Anhui Come to Shanghai to Beg for Relief 145

The Northern Anhui 21-County Water Disaster Aftermath Committee has elected Gao Weixuan, Chen Ziheng, Yang Yaonan, and Li Zhuxi as representatives to go to Beijing and Shanghai to beg for relief. It is learned that the representatives have arrived in Beijing from Bengbu and petitioned various agencies. They came to Shanghai yesterday and presented documents to the National Government Water Disaster Relief Association, the Relief Committee, the Shanghai Fundraising Association for Emergency Relief of Water Disasters in Various Provinces, the Anhui Water Disaster Relief Association, the Sino-Foreign Relief Association, the Red Cross Society, the Jisheng Association, and various charitable organizations. They wrote that this year's flood disaster was particularly severe in Anhui, especially in the 21 counties in northern Anhui, which are located in a remote corner along the Huai River. The disaster area is more than 800 miles long. Because the electric poles were broken and the shipping was suspended, transportation was gradually cut off, and communication was interrupted. The people along the Huai River are struggling to survive and have no time to promote their plight. Therefore, the outside world knows little about it, unlike the Wuhan disaster, which was witnessed by people from China and abroad. The breaches of the Wuhu weirs in southern Anhui have received special attention from the provincial government. It is found that Anhui Province is listed as a severely affected province this year, and the 21 counties in northern Anhui, where the Huai River overflowed and formed a swamp, are indeed severely affected. Therefore, people from China and abroad agree that the first batch of 170,000 yuan allocated by the National Government for emergency relief was allocated by the Anhui Province Relief Commissioner without detailed investigation. The relief was distributed in the provincial capital. The 20 counties in central and southern Anhui received 90,000 yuan in relief funds, while the 21 counties in northern Anhui only received 50,000 yuan. Only the 53 counties of Shouhuo and the town of Linhuai received practical benefits. The other counties all suffered from a lack of assistance. However, it can be said that during the height of the flood, emergency relief was difficult to extend. The relief officials and the investigators sent by the provincial government were unable to conduct field investigations due to traffic obstruction or time constraints. Therefore, the distribution of emergency relief was not average. Winter and spring relief can be a second step to remedy this. Disaster relief is related to the lives of the people, and the relief personnel bear a heavy responsibility. They cannot determine the severity of the disaster based on the presence or absence of publicity. Those in charge of Anhui did not conduct a thorough investigation beforehand, nor did they hear of any remedial measures afterward. The second distribution of relief funds took the first as an example. According to the truth, how can it be said to be fair? Recently, various counties in northern Anhui have reported to the association that the entire disaster area in northern Anhui, whether the counties along the Huai River or the low-lying areas of the tributaries of the Huai River, are still flooded. It is not difficult to ask for the dispatch of commissioners to investigate each county. The representatives have been entrusted with the heavy responsibility of the disaster victims in each county, and they feel terrified at night. They have always admired your association's compassion and treated everyone equally. You are very concerned about the disaster situation in Anhui, and the disaster situation in northern Anhui is more severe than in southern and central Anhui. It is expected that you have long been aware of it. It is reasonable to base it on the facts, represent the public opinion, and believe that the relief funds for northern Anhui should not be distributed equally with those for central and southern Anhui. The reasons are written and sincerely request your association to send personnel to investigate thoroughly and provide prompt relief to value the lives of the people and show fairness. We are extremely urgent and await your orders.

News on Printing the Song Dynasty Buddhist Canon 148

General Zhu Ziqiao's Grand Ambition

To be undertaken by the Buddhist Studies Bookstore

The only remaining Zhu-printed Buddhist complete canon in our country is still stored in the Wolong Temple and Xian Temple in Xi'an. Kang Nanhai wanted to reproduce it by photocopying but failed. Indeed, this great canon is the only precious treasure in our country. Last year, General Zhu Ziqiao released relief to Shaanxi, saw it, and was pleasantly surprised. He urgently wanted to reproduce and circulate it, and he discussed it with believers in various places who were very enthusiastic. This year, he came to Shanghai and had earnest discussions with religious and charitable circles in Shanghai. After several meetings, it was decided to use lithography to print a quarto edition, each copy costing about 500 yuan, which is ten times cheaper than the Qing Dynasty Dragon Canon and can obtain a Song Dynasty carved edition. It is expected that circulation will be very prosperous. It is reported that the book has been decided to be undertaken by the Buddhist Studies Bookstore in this city.

Ma Er, the Murderer in the Smuggling Case, Still Tries to Deny It 149

He Robbed Property and Injured Two Lives. The Witness's Testimony is Conclusive. The Judge Says, "Your Conscience is Too Bad."

Ma Er, a Tongzhou native and the rickshaw driver of Cai Zhitian, a Chinese detective at the Huishan Police Station, gathered accomplices and went to the western-style house on the second floor of Yichang Electric Company, 196 East Seward Road, at about 1 a.m. on the 19th of last month. They killed Gu Cao, Zhu's relative, and Zhou Lushi, the maid, and robbed jewelry worth more than 1,000 yuan. After the case was discovered, Ma was sent to the First Special District Court for interrogation. Details have been reported in this newspaper. The police station summoned witnesses and the owner the day before yesterday and sent Ma Er again to the Fifth Criminal Court for investigation. Zhang Tianyin, the lawyer for the police station, stated that there were two witnesses who could prove that the blood-stained clothes seized were worn by Ma in the past. The date was changed to bail out the original stolen goods, a coat made of Yuan silk and satin fur, from a certain pawnshop for 8 yuan. The clothes, the white cloth belt worn by Ma (because there were blood spots), the short-sleeved shirt with blood stains, the murder weapon, etc., were presented for inspection. According to Zhu Yangshan, a native of Qingpu, Gu Cao, the victim, was his maternal aunt, and Zhou Lushi was a maid. At the time of the incident, he had gone to Wuxi on business and returned to Shanghai on the 20th. He observed that the thieves had entered from the rear of the house by dismantling the fence at the top of the wall. More than 1,000 yuan of property was robbed. As for the 500 yuan in banknotes, there was no such amount. The three-year-old child who had not suffered was Gu Cao's son. He had never met the defendant before. The child pointed to the window, saying "that afternoon", etc. According to Cai, the detective, the defendant had been a rickshaw driver at his place for more than eleven months. He did not work badly in the past, but suddenly changed recently. After the incident, he looked panicked. A blood-stained short-sleeved shirt with a patched place was found in Zhu's house. He recalled that Ma usually wore it, and that's how he was arrested. There are now two witnesses in court who can testify. However, when searching his bedroom after the incident, there were no stolen goods or silver dollars. He went out for three nights between the 10th and 20th of last month, and it is not known what he was doing. According to Xiao Cao, who worked as a laundryman at Cai's detective office, he washed the blood-stained short-sleeved shirt three times, so he recognized it without error. In the past, he could eat three or four bowls of rice per meal, but after the incident, he only ate one bowl, a significant decrease. He was asked to sign a statement. According to Gu Afu, who worked as a rickshaw driver at Shi Huanting's detective office at the Huishan Police Station, he saw Ma every day when he went to the police station and talked and laughed. He saw a hole in the pocket of the white cloth short-sleeved shirt he was wearing, which was the blood-stained clothes presented in court. After speaking, he was also asked to sign a statement. When questioned, Ma Er firmly denied that the blood-stained clothes belonged to him and tried to deny it in every possible way. Judge Shen Bingrong declared that this case was indeed a case of "Heaven's net is wide, and though its meshes are coarse, nothing can slip through." He was arrested because of the clothes. Otherwise, he would still be at large. "You have a very bad conscience. You robbed property and injured two lives. There is no need to deny it now. Confess who the mastermind is or who fooled you so that you can reduce your sentence." Ma Er categorically denied it. According to Banas, the Western detective of the General Department, on the 25th of last month, he and Chief Detective Mike, Chinese Detective Tang Jian, and Detective Cai went to the victim's home with the defendant, who pointed out where he had entered, and the details of killing the two women, robbing the clothes, packing them in a box, and first going out to see if there were any patrols, etc. There was no coercion, etc. Judge Shen instructed that he should be sent back into custody and rescheduled for another hearing.

Tianjin Woman Asks for Mediation to Break Away from Family Relationship 151

Unable to Bear the Abuse of the Eldest Wife, Both Parties Agreed to Mediation.

Liang Guizhen, a woman from Tianjin, hired a lawyer to file a petition with the Mediation Court of the Second Special District Court to request to break away from the family relationship of her husband, Li Zhengzhi. The petition for mediation is recorded as follows: "Unable to bear the trampling of women, the authority of the eldest wife, and the abuse of the husband, I request mediation to break away from the family relationship. I, the petitioner, lost my mother at the age of three and my father at the age of twelve. At the age of sixteen, I was controlled by the old family and married to the respondent due to the sweet talk of my late mother and matchmaker. When the marriage was discussed, it was claimed to be the original match, but unexpectedly, three days after entering the door, the respondent's eldest wife came from Shandong to Tianjin and lived with the petitioner. At that time, the petitioner knew that she was weak in knowledge and encountered misfortune, but the die was cast, and the rice was cooked. It was useless to cry out in vain. Thinking late at night, I sighed that my fate was thin and hated who to blame. I only hoped that the respondent would be considerate and try to comfort me. My lifelong grievances could also be resolved. How could I expect that the petitioner's thoughts were so, but the opposite was true? Not long after the marriage, I moved to Shanghai with the eldest wife. Then the respondent was unemployed and in difficulty, so he pawned and borrowed money to make a living, which led to a high debt platform, and often beat the petitioner for no reason, and the eldest wife helped to cheer, arbitrarily insulting. Under this tyranny, several years have passed. Now the respondent is accustomed to humiliation and has become more and more tyrannical. On the 19th of last month, I was beaten severely again, and the petitioner went to Heji Hospital for treatment. There is now an injury certificate to prove it. He thinks of women as toys, oblivious to pity, and the eldest wife treats the petitioner as inferior, almost like a servant. How can I endure this life? I have no choice but to request permission to break away from the family relationship." The court, according to the petition, summoned both parties to court for mediation the day before yesterday. According to Liang Guizhen, she is twenty-one years old this year and married the respondent at the age of sixteen. After entering the door, she unexpectedly learned that the respondent already had an eldest wife. At that time, the woman thought that the die was cast, so she endured it. However, she was often subjected to various abuses by her husband and the eldest wife, and the real situation made it impossible to live together. Therefore, I came to the case to request separation, etc. When asked, Li Zhengzhi, a native of Shandong, stated that he is now practicing medicine at 96 Yongyu Lane, West Gate Road. Five years ago, he married the petitioner as his wife, and there is an official marriage certificate to prove it. After moving to Shanghai and living together, his wife often went out alone on the pretext of watching a movie and returned home late at night. Therefore, the merchant has repeatedly scolded her, but he has not dared to abuse her. The petitioner's request for separation is difficult to accept. I request that the petitioner be ordered to return home and live together. Judge Qu persuaded both parties for a while, and as a result, both parties agreed to reschedule the mediation, and the court approved it.

Search and Seizure of the American Merchants Association 152

Gamblers are dealt with separately. Dancing men and women were not arrested.

The Mainland Daily reports that after midnight on the 10th, the public concession Xinzha and Jing'an Temple police stations dispatched patrols, led by Assistant Chief Inspector McGivray, to search the International Merchants Association at 90 Tongfu Road. Many Westerners were gambling with a foreign gambling tool. Eight gamblers from Britain, Denmark, and Japan provided their names and addresses and were allowed to go home. Twenty-five Russian men and women were taken back to the Xinzha Police Station and each ordered to provide 500 yuan bail before being released pending trial. There were still fifty people dancing downstairs who were not arrested.

Passenger Dies Suddenly 153

The night before last, at 10 p.m., a guest died suddenly in room 152 of the Dadong Hotel on Nanjing Road. The police were notified, and the body was sent to Renji Hospital for examination. The deceased was reportedly surnamed Yu, named Le, 40 years old, a native of Guangdong, and had been living there for many days. He had a friend surnamed Liang who came and went from time to time.

Tea Servant Injured Fingers Picking Up Can 154

The injury was very minor. He was bandaged and discharged from the hospital.

At about 10:10 last night, Zhang Jinrong (38 years old), a tea servant from Pinghu, was walking past the entrance of the Nanjing Grand Theater on Edouard Road when he saw a can that looked like a cigarette tin on the side of the road. His curiosity was aroused, and he picked it up and looked at it for a long time. Then, he lifted the lid of the can, and suddenly there was a loud bang. It exploded immediately. Fortunately, the force was not very strong, and only his fingers were slightly injured. He was found by a nearby patrolman and sent to the Songshan Road Police Station and then to the hospital. Because the injury was very minor, he was bandaged and discharged from the hospital immediately.

Carpenter Fell and Died 155

Flats are being demolished and built near Zhaofeng Road in the public concession, contracted by Lv Shunji Construction Factory. Yesterday afternoon at 3:30, a carpenter named Shu Sheng fell off the ladder and fell. He hit a lead bucket on the lower level with his abdomen, causing his large intestine to bleed. He lost consciousness. The workers helped him up and threw him up and down hard in the hope of waking him up. However, his internal injuries were too severe, and he died. The body was sent to Tongren Hospital and then to the morgue for examination, pending a report to the court for handling.

Another Imposter Soliciting Donations 156

Previously, a certain person, identified as Person A, went to Room 7 of the company building at 371 Avenue Albert, in the French Concession, to solicit donations from a Westerner, Mr. Mamuya. Person A claimed to be a staff member of the Nanjing Buddhist Orphanage and that the orphanage was facing financial difficulties, so he was appealing to philanthropists from all walks of life to support the cause. Mr. Mamuya immediately asked Person A about his occupation. Person A, upon hearing that Mr. Mamuya worked in the political department of the police station, became evasive and hastily took his leave. Mr. Mamuya was very suspicious and immediately sent a letter of inquiry to the Nanjing Buddhist Orphanage. The orphanage has now replied: "Respectfully, we received your letter inquiring whether our orphanage has sent anyone to Shanghai to solicit donations. In response, we have investigated and found that our orphanage has never sent anyone to Shanghai to solicit donations. If anyone is found impersonating us to commit fraud, we hope that you will immediately investigate and arrest them for severe punishment, to deter such wicked practices. We would be most grateful. This is a special reply. We hope you will take note of this. To the Special Political Department of the French Police Station. Nanjing Buddhist Orphanage. October 9th," and so on. Recently, the decline of moral standards and the prevalence of swindling have been frequently reported. The French Concession authorities have now ordered all police detectives to thoroughly investigate and arrest such individuals and hand them over to the nearest police station for severe punishment.

Daytime Fire on Miller Road 157

At around 3:00 PM the day before yesterday, a fire broke out at house numbers 9 to 15 on Miller Road, Wuchang Road. Initially, the fire was extremely fierce, with flames spreading in all directions, making it impossible to approach. The fire spread to the Long Kee Bicycle Shop, Xin Da Shoe Store, Tong Kee Printing Press, etc., at the corner of Wuchang Road, numbers 944 to 945, causing significant losses. The India Hotel, Qian Pi Hao (dry goods store), and Wang Wen Kee Clothing Store were also affected. A total of seven buildings were destroyed. When the fire broke out, the Hongkou Fire Brigade received the news and immediately rushed to the scene to extinguish the fire. The fire was finally extinguished at around 4:30 PM.

Fire at Seafood Store 158

The Zhen Ru Seafood Store at 176-177 Route des Soeurs (Avenue Dubail) in the Chinese-French Border Area caught fire suddenly on the mezzanine floor at 9:30 AM yesterday morning. Flames burst through the roof, damaging goods such as shark fins, fish maw, and sea cucumbers, with losses estimated at over two thousand yuan. The mezzanine floor was also destroyed. The fire brigade rushed to the scene and extinguished the fire.

Mr. Lang Deshan, a renowned Chinese artist who has toured the world and enjoys great fame, along with his beloved daughter and over ten performers, has now set off from New York to return to China. Mr. Lang once returned to China four years ago and was warmly welcomed by the people. He then traveled to Australia and other places, including all countries in Oceania and North America. This time, he will return to China to perform his new contributions.

Record of the Annual General Meeting of the Shaoxing Fellow-Countrymen Association 161

The Shaoxing Fellow-Countrymen Association in Shanghai, located at 26 Aierjin Road, held its 21st Annual General Meeting on October 10th. The meeting was chaired by the President, Wang Xiaolai, who reported the purpose of the meeting. He then stated that the association had previously received orders from the Shanghai Municipal Party Department and the Social Affairs Bureau to revise its constitution, prepare registers, and submit them for registration. The Municipal Party Department and the Social Affairs Bureau approved the instructions, but the constitution was deemed unsuitable and returned for revision. The Board of Directors has now resolved to submit the constitution for approval at the Annual General Meeting and then re-elect the executive and supervisory committee members. It is now proposed to discuss the thirty-two articles of the constitution, and members present are requested to amend and approve them. It was also resolved to establish a committee and elect the executive and supervisory committee members within the shortest possible time to comply with legal requirements. It is reported that the election will be held in early November.

Reader's Correspondence

Mr. Zhang Xutang (The Fundamental Blueprint for Resistance and National Salvation) 163

People must insult themselves before others insult them. Is not the current forceful occupation of the Northeast by the violent Japanese due to our country's endless internal strife, inviting humiliation upon ourselves? Like a bolt from the blue, awakening from a deep sleep, our compatriots now know that without resistance and national salvation, there is no way to survive. However, upon detailed examination, where exactly lies the weakness of our compatriots? It is none other than the selfish and self-interested thoughts and behaviors engendered by the ancient inherited concepts of family and individual. The concept of selfishness and self-interest has deeply penetrated the hearts of the people. Furthermore, with the economic oppression from foreign countries and the increasingly difficult social life, the concept of selfishness and self-interest is becoming increasingly rampant, to the point that all compatriots throughout the country only know how to create personal comfort, raise offspring in luxury, and ensure the family's wealth and honor for generations, while regarding the chaos and decline of the country and society and the poverty and suffering of compatriots as irrelevant. Alas, in this world of the survival of the fittest, what kind of strength and achievements can be expected from a nation of selfish and self-interested people who organize a government and maintain society? Therefore, if the Chinese people want to resist Japan and save the country today, they must first abolish this evil concept. In the past, all compatriots, regardless of their background, should ask themselves honestly whether they have made mistakes. In the face of national crisis, as long as they awaken and repent from now on, all past debts should be forgiven (except for unrepentant communists). Starting anew, everyone should vow to unite as one, moving forward on the path of great impartiality, mutual assistance, mutual love, and shared existence and prosperity. Only then can the nation have hope for self-strengthening. However, to achieve this goal, it is essential to publicly define a common goal to serve as a model and example for promotion and common adherence. I hereby propose the following in brief, and I hope to discuss them with compatriots throughout the country: (1) All adult male and female citizens of the Republic of China who have a legitimate occupation, such as education, writing, journalism, labor, agriculture, military, politics, law, industry, and commerce, etc., and whose character is upright, scholarship is excellent, who are free from the various vices of smoking, gambling, and prostitution, whose lives are frugal, whose words and actions are consistent, who are mutually helpful and loving, who prioritize the public over the private, who prioritize the country over the family, and who in all matters take the shared existence and prosperity of compatriots as a prerequisite, especially those who are enthusiastic about education, writing, and journalism, and who are determined to build models and lay foundations for the country and the nation, these compatriots are truly the pillars of the country and the teachers of the people and should be given special respect and preferential treatment. Other compatriots who can each do their best and contribute their talents to their occupations, devoting themselves wholeheartedly and striving for progress and development, and who have various inventions and achievements that benefit the country, the nation, and society, are excellent citizens, and all compatriots throughout the country should respect and cherish them. (2) All adult male and female citizens of the Republic of China who have no legitimate occupation, or who have an occupation but engage in the following behaviors, such as having immoral conduct, "smoking, gambling, prostitution, various vices," relying on laziness, being selfish and self-interested, making absurd statements, deceiving and cheating, being cunning and malicious, fabricating rumors and sowing discord, manipulating and exploiting, harming the country and the people, and all kinds of behaviors that violate the common existence of compatriots in order to achieve their personal goals of stealing fame and reputation, obtaining promotions and wealth, enjoying comfort and luxury, and keeping concubines, these people are the vermin of our compatriots and the scum of humanity, especially those who use education, writing, and journalism to seek personal gain, those who use military, political, and legal power to oppress and exploit compatriots, and those unscrupulous merchants and corrupt monks who use commerce to solicit shares and raise capital, engage in embezzlement and corruption, and seek lucky opportunities for speculation, who, when they fail, remain unpunished by the law (the law does not restrain them, and society does not condemn them, so that people dare not invest in various industries), are evil citizens, and all compatriots throughout the country should investigate, monitor, and severely condemn them at any time, urging them to awaken and repent. If they are inherently vicious and stubborn to the point of death, then their crimes and misdeeds should be announced, and the government should be requested to severely punish and execute them. If this cannot be achieved, then compatriots throughout the country should rise up to sanction and abandon them, striving to ensure that these selfish, self-interested, harmful, and misleading evil citizens disappear from the Republic of China in this time of crisis and survival. My compatriots, my beloved compatriots, think about it, think deeply about it. The bankruptcy of our country's education today, the corruption of politics, the arrogance of the military, the snobbery of scholars, the extravagance of the rich, the poverty of laborers and farmers, the failure of unscrupulous merchants to seek excellence and durability in their products, the substitution of domestic goods by counterfeiters using inferior goods, and all kinds of deceitful, fraudulent, immoral, and shameless behaviors in society are all the result of the concept of family and individual selfishness. The Communist Party's terrorist policies, acts of killing and slaughter, we oppose them extremely because they extinguish humanity, but if we do not follow the trend, thoroughly awaken, and abolish our own evil thoughts and behaviors of enjoying abundant food and beautiful clothes, being happy and carefree, and not caring about the life and death of others, and strive to make the deformed and unequal society become increasingly equal, then the collapse is only a matter of time. My beloved scholars, rich people, intelligent and clever people, if you do not quickly catch up, awaken those who are unaware, and work together to change selfishness and self-interest into mutual assistance and mutual benefit, and change self-respect and self-indulgence into shared respect and shared excellence, then our Chinese nation, even without the invasion of the Japanese pirates, will be difficult to escape the disturbances of the communist bandits and will perish. Do you not see that today, the great disaster of national subjugation and racial extinction is already upon us, and yet the party and state gentlemen who bear the responsibility of saving the country and the people are still arguing over conditions, giving the Japanese slaves the opportunity to sow discord and fabricate rumors? The state is the barrier of the nation, and the government is the base camp for the common survival of the people. It is necessary to ensure that politics are enlightened, right and wrong are commonly seen, and society is at peace, so that the work of resisting Japan and saving the country can be thorough. Only then can our Chinese nation have hope of revival.

Floating Life News (Methods for Counter Staff and Workers to Boycott Japanese Goods on Their Own)

Recently read Bingyuan’s News, boycotting inferior goods is the first good method to save the country and no addition. Repeated boycotts have resulted in failure, all because of unscrupulous merchants seeking profit. As Bingyuan said, although there are enthusiastic comrades who are determined not to buy inferior goods, most unscrupulous merchants only know how to seek profit and do not care about national demise. They clearly label inferior goods as domestic goods, so buyers do not realize it. I serve in the cloth industry and firmly believe that this is true. Now, the only solution is for workers in various industries to boycott on their own. For example, counter staff should not sell inferior goods, and workers should not transport inferior goods. But there are two difficulties: (1) As counter staff, they are forced under the power of capitalists, and all actions are not free. (2) Workers are all from poor families and are limited by their livelihoods and have no choice but to compromise in order to make a living. Fortunately, Mingjiao responded in the newspaper,

(Reply) Change selfishness and self-interest into mutual assistance and mutual benefit, change self-respect and self-indulgence into shared respect and shared excellence. Zhang's hope, if it can really be achieved, that would be extremely good. In this time of national crisis, probably all parties have some awareness, but just being aware is not enough; everyone must start from their own selves. So we often say to people, if you feel that something should be done, you must do it yourself first, and if you feel that something should not be done, you must not do it yourself first. Otherwise, Zhang said that even without the invasion of Japan, we will inevitably be disturbed and destroyed by the communist bandits, which is absolutely true. Floating Life's suggestion to boycott the issue and advocate that counter staff and workers boycott on their own is indeed a fundamental solution. Afraid of being oppressed by capitalists and involving livelihood issues, I think capitalists also have a conscience, and everyone loves their country as much as I do. Let us try our best to persuade and guide them.

Weather Report 165

The Xujiahui Observatory's weather forecast at 4:30 PM yesterday stated that the Yangtze River basin and coastal areas are cloudy and cold, with some areas clearing up. There are strong northeasterly winds in the Yellow Sea and the East China Sea. The weather around Ryukyu is bad due to the hurricane, which has apparently turned north. The hurricane's position at around 11:00 AM in the morning was within 120 miles of the intersection of 21 degrees north latitude and 130 degrees east longitude, and it was turning north. Another was within 120 miles of the intersection of 34 degrees north latitude and 145 degrees east longitude, heading northeast. Also, in the 24 hours before 3:00 PM yesterday, the highest temperature in Shanghai was 69.4 degrees and the lowest was 56.7 degrees. On the same day last year, the highest was 74.3 degrees and the lowest was 53.4 degrees.

Great China University: Great China University held a solemn and fervent National Day Commemoration Meeting at 9:00 AM on the 10th. Over a thousand faculty members and students attended. After the ceremony, Vice President Ou Yuanhuai gave a speech, stating that today's meeting was not so much to commemorate National Day as it was to commemorate national crisis, national mourning, and national humiliation. Recognizing the urgency of the current disaster, we should begin today by deeply repenting, deeply awakening, and working together to strive for effective national salvation efforts to jointly plan the nation's revival. Then, Chen Binhe, director of the Japanese Studies Society, gave a speech on the issue of violent Japanese aggression in the Northeast, and Zhang Ke Wei, a professor from Northeastern University, spoke about the situation of Shenyang being occupied. Finally, representatives from the faculty and staff, as well as representatives from various departments, delivered speeches successively, and dispersed after shouting slogans together.

Nanyang Commercial High School: The volunteer army of Nanyang Commercial High School on Tiantong'an Road has achieved outstanding results since its establishment. Yesterday, on Double Tenth Day, the school held a military parade. Several hundred student soldiers, all wearing black uniforms, used wooden guns newly ordered from the Commercial Press. Under the command of military instructor He Xinliang, the military appearance was neat and orderly. Two hundred female students, all serving as nursing teams. Organizing a National Salvation Fund Custody Committee

(5) Other important matters.

(Resolution) Elect representatives from Fudan Affiliated Middle School, Hujiang Affiliated Middle School, Youth Middle School, Minli Middle School, Wuben Girls' Middle School, Huizhong Middle School, and Guanghua Affiliated Middle School to serve as members of the National Salvation Fund Custody Committee. (3) A telegram to the central government requesting the immediate promulgation of concrete policies toward Japan. (Resolution) To be drafted by the executive committee. (4) Inspecting the case of middle school students frequenting entertainment venues. (Resolution) To be formulated by the executive committee. (5) A notice to students of all middle schools to hold a swearing-in ceremony to refuse cooperation with Japan. (Resolution) Passed. (6) Appointing three representatives to go to Nanjing to request the central government to issue firearms. (Resolution) Passed. The candidates will be nominated by the executive committee. (7) What to do if the school authorities do not implement the cases discussed by this conference. (Resolution) Request the Municipal Education Bureau and the Municipal Party Department to be the backing. (8) The funding of this conference. (Resolution) Each school will pay ten yuan, and more will be raised if necessary.

Teachers and Students Who Have Left the School Must Return Quickly

Jinan University, because of its efforts in the anti-Japanese national salvation movement, had its classes interrupted and changed. Now, all teachers and students, recognizing that the situation has a protracted nature, and based on the principle of saving the country through academics, have decided to resume normal operations and regular classes in the Great China and Secondary Departments starting today, and to work hard on military training and propaganda in the morning and evening. All teachers and students who have left the school for personal reasons are expected to return to the school quickly to cancel their leave; otherwise, they will be treated as suspended or dismissed after the specified deadline.

THE HISTORY OF THE QIU-LIN BATTLE 179

Three to one... Qiu beats Lin

Qiu Feihai 6|6 6|3 3|2 8|6 Lin Baohua

In the country, when talking about tennis, people admire Lin Baohua and Qiu Feihai. It can be said that the skills of these two are unparalleled in the country. Three years ago, Lin once defeated Qiu, and Lin's position surpassed Qiu's. Later, the two went their separate ways, separated north and south. The changes in the skills of each became a topic of conversation after drinking tea and wine in recent years. Until the National Day, after Qiu Feihai defeated Lin Baohua three to one, today's Qiu has undoubtedly leaped ahead of Lin. Although the two are national players, there is no need to keep their wins and losses in mind. I hope they will not abandon themselves, strive for progress, and promote future generations to open up a new world. The future of Chinese tennis is really promising.

ART EACH HAS ITS OWN MERITS 丨 180

Being experienced, steady, and winning can be regarded as a memorable page in Qiu's life's record. At the opening of the war, Qiu was trapped under Lin's racket, and his eyes were full of thorns, and he was unable to recover. Every time he thought of extricating himself, he found it difficult to do so. The balls he hit were often soaked, leading to the failure of the first set. At that time, Qiu's will was calm, and he obviously had the demeanor of a great general. He was experienced and steady in drawing the ball at the corner, which was accurate and powerful. He tried to save the second set easily and took the third set. In the fourth set, which was a matter of life and death, Lin led several times, seeming to be able to take it as his own, but Qiu was always able to fight against it. At that time, if there was any slackness, he would be hit hard. After four intense sets, Qiu was already exhausted. If the game was extended, all his efforts would be wasted. Qiu knew himself and his enemy, so he could win the final victory. After the battle, he fell to the ground, showing that Qiu's victory was not easy. Strategic errors: Lin has two major advantages: 1. He is powerful in serving and especially good at blocking the net. 2. He is young, strong, and tireless in long battles, but he is prone to anger when frustrated, which is his biggest problem. Winning the first set too easily aroused a sense of complacency, and he abandoned his best skills in grabbing the net and insisted on long shots. The strategy was not his strength. He mistakenly lost the second and third sets to others. In the fourth set, Lin's muscles were strong and he looked much better. If he remained calm, he could have won, and the fifth set could have been predicted to go to Lin. But his anger had already spread, and his ability to restrain himself was weak. He failed and destroyed himself. Qiu had his own strengths in winning, and Lin should know the focus of his failure.

GOLD PRICES PLUMMETED LAST WEEK DUE TO THE AIR 186

Down forty-nine taels. Last week, the mark gold suddenly turned sluggish, with drastic changes. The market was like a raging storm, not to be approached, with daily fluctuations of more than twenty taels. Initially at seven hundred and twenty taels, it then broke through seven hundred taels. It was indeed due to the trend of rising silver prices and rising exchange rates. Traders tended to sell British and American exchange rates to hedge. It is estimated that British gold has exceeded one shilling and eight pence, and American gold is outside thirty-three yuan. People were extremely terrified, especially because the United States was planning to convene a silver conference, and the Japanese political situation was turbulent. Furthermore, the Japanese pirates in the East Province were invading one after another. The high price at the beginning of this week was seven hundred and twenty-nine taels, and the closing price on the weekend was suddenly six hundred and seventy-eight and a half taels, with a total difference of fifty taels and five cents, a total drop of forty-nine taels. According to the settlement price of the US exchange rate, it was sixty taels to ninety taels, and finally more than eighty taels. Generally, the bulls and bears controlled each other, but there was no certainty, because they were subject to the influence of the air. However, there is still a dramatic change in the future. However, I am afraid that the bulls will rarely win. The following is a summary of the progress of this week:

The daily ups and downs began on Monday (October 5). The big bar silver increased by 4,375, the silver price increased by 125, the shilling increased by two files, and the internal market was also loose. Traders were selling, and the hedge was like the US dollar leaving thirty-two or three taels. The gold market opened at seven hundred and twenty-seven taels, down five and a half taels, then twenty-nine taels. Later, it gradually fell further and further, with a strong selling trend. It was also heard that the United States was planning to use both gold and silver, so it fell sharply by more than ten taels, or twelve taels. The noon closing price was fifteen taels. In the afternoon, it opened at fifteen and a half taels, but it rose to twenty-two taels because of more purchases. The closing price was sixteen taels and six cents, down fifteen taels and nine cents from last Saturday. The front and back markets had a total of seventeen taels of rotation. A large household, Mr. Wu, advanced and retreated. The next day, the big bar increased by another 875, the silver price also increased by 875, the shilling increased by three files, and the internal market rebounded. It was a state of tightness, and traders were paying shillings and selling US dollars. Yesterday, in the gold market, the opening price dropped by eleven taels and six cents to seven hundred and five taels, then to zero four taels and five cents. Later, because the big bar was still in good condition, the United States sold it, and the market turned soft. Furthermore, there was fear that the British and American exchange rates would rebound, so the big bar might fall back. People's hearts were easily moved, so the gold price gradually rose, soaring by more than ten taels to sixteen taels and eight cents. The noon closing price was fourteen taels and one cent. In the afternoon, the market opened at fifteen and a half taels and then showed a good situation, reaching twenty-four taels and two cents. The closing price was twenty-four taels, a rebound of seven taels and four cents. The whole day had a nineteen taels and seven cents rotation. On Wednesday, the big bar shrank from 375 to 4375, and the US silver also decreased by 125. The shilling did not change, and the internal market was flat. Traders in the gold industry were selling, because the US dollar was harder and the shilling seemed soft. As for the mark gold, the opening price was seven hundred and twenty taels, down four taels. Then, it went from nineteen taels to twenty-one taels. Although the big bar shrank, the silver price was not enough. Furthermore, there was talk of the United States saving the silver price issue by reconvening the conference. The big households sold heavily, and the price plunged by more than ten taels, breaking into seven hundred and ten taels, or zero seven taels. The noon closing price rebounded to twelve taels and two cents, and the Indian exchange rate reported small. The next day, the big bar did not change, the silver price increased by 375, the shilling was as before, the US dollar was small, due to the exchange rate relationship, and the internal market increased. However, it was chaotic, and the industry was selling to hedge. The gold market at seven hundred and four taels and five already added seven taels and two cents. Securities: Last Week's Bond Price Fluctuations Remain Severe 189

Compared to the Previous Week, the Decline Was Even Greater

Only 1929 Customs Bonds Were Relatively Stable

Last week (from October 5th to 10th), the bond market conditions in this city's securities market were as usual, except for Saturday's National Day holiday. Spot transactions were scarce. Although many types were available, the total turnover was only 26,000 yuan. The futures market was also quite quiet. The November futures contracts started trading on Thursday. The total turnover for the week was 53.255 million yuan, an increase of about 23 million yuan compared to the previous week. As for the fluctuations, they were still very severe. On Monday, due to the lack of improvement in the diplomatic situation, the market was weak and prices fell steadily. Except for the 1936 bonds, and the 1929 customs bonds, which fell by four yuan and trading was suspended, all other bonds fell by two, three, or three yuan. On Tuesday, the situation was dull, and there was news of a peaceful resolution with Guangdong, which improved market sentiment slightly. Short positions were covered, and the supply and demand situation was somewhat balanced. Prices fluctuated without a major decline. On Wednesday, the situation became tense again, with active selling transactions from all sides. Bond prices fell across the board. The Disbandment 1929 Customs Bonds were suspended from trading again due to excessive decline. Other bonds also fell by small amounts, such as three or four yuan. The 1936 bonds also fell by six jiao. On Thursday, the market situation suddenly changed. Although there was no significant improvement in the diplomatic situation, due to the substantial decline in recent days, and the financial industry's joint discussions on maintaining stability, the market became more active for a time. Many short positions were covered, and retail investors actively invested. The morning market gradually strengthened. Investor sentiment was even better in the afternoon, with prices soaring and trading being suspended due to demand exceeding supply. Only a few types of bonds, such as the Customs Tariff Reorganization 1936 bonds, were not suspended from trading. However, this sudden surge was purely due to temporary investor enthusiasm. Therefore, on Friday, buyers became hesitant, and bond prices fell sharply. For example, the 1920 Customs Bonds and the Consolidated Tax 1929 Bonds fell to the limit price in the early morning and trading was suspended. The Disbandment 1929 Customs Bonds and the Salt Tax Bonds were also suspended from trading in the afternoon. By the time the market closed, the trend had started to ease, and the after-hours trading of bonds showed slight increases after the declines. As a result, compared to the previous week, the Disbandment Bonds fell by more than ten yuan, the 1920 Customs Bonds also fell by more than eight yuan, and the Reorganization, Consolidated Tax, and Salt Tax Bonds also fell by more than six yuan. Only the 1929 Customs Bonds fell slightly by seven or eight jiao. The spot prices of the whole 1936, the disbandment, the 1920 roll tax, and other items have not been compared for a long time, and the spot prices have fallen by more than ten yuan compared with last month. The bond market may be temporarily stable. If the diplomatic situation does not deteriorate further, it is hoped that it will gradually strengthen. Cotton Yarn: Overseas Cotton Telegrams for the Past Two Days

American, British, and Egyptian Cotton Are All Strong... Only Indian Cotton Fell

On the 9th, the American cotton market was mixed. Reactive buying strengthened it, but increased receipts weakened it. Futures fell by 1 to 3 points, and spot prices fell by 5 points. British cotton futures rose by 8 or 9 points, and spot prices rose by 8 points. Egyptian cotton spot prices rose by 10 points. Indian cotton was sold by Japanese merchants and bought by Indian investors. The market was calm and firm. Bengals rose by 2.5 rupees, Oomras rose by 2.75 rupees, and Broach rose by 2 rupees. On the 10th, the American cotton market was stable. At the close, it surged due to buying by brokers and the public. Futures rose by 10 to 14 points, and spot prices rose by 15 points. British cotton futures fell by 1 point, and spot prices fell by 6 points. Egyptian cotton spot prices fell by 5 points. Indian cotton initially fell slightly with American cotton, but later softened due to profit-taking by bulls. Bengals fell by 2.75 rupees, and Oomras and Broach both fell by 3.25 rupees. Grain and Rice Market Trends Upward 191

In Shanghai South, there were about 50 boats from the west road source in the past two days. The early rice of the kiln type was lacking, and nearly a thousand stones of cargo from the middle pass of the river were brought in. The entire amount was sold out that day, and the price also increased by 0.2 to 0.3 yuan. Due to the relationship between the cost of letters from the mainland, the supply will definitely be short. The new japonica rice and the new reed tip rice were scarce, and the price was also tightly pulled. The influence of the new goods on the rice husking is difficult to increase the market. The price of white rice with pointed leaves is still the same, and the market is changing in a negative direction. The wine merchants are very light, and the downstream is also very low.

Xinzha: Yesterday's market trend was rising. The River bottom was more lively than the previous market. The top-quality Changxi new japonica rice and the middle-quality white japonica rice were each offered at a price increase of 0.1 to 0.2 yuan. The new Baige rice also increased by 0.1 yuan. Although there was early and late rice on the stack, the number was not large. The opening price was fixed. The sales of new yang Du tip rice and white rice with pointed leaves are slowing down. The overall market is stable, and the transaction of foreign rice in this city is limited. The price of transshipment gangs is rising slightly. Glutinous rice has arrived and is being sold slowly, and the situation has declined by nearly one jiao. There were about 70 boats in total.

Sugar Market: Tate & Lyle Sugar is Scarce and in Demand 192

Yesterday's sugar market, due to the fact that it was a Sunday and there was no telegram from the production area, the association market was divided. The price of Dutch coarse sand white was still set at 11 taels per piece. The price of newly arrived goods that could not be shipped was 11 taels, 3 qian and 5 fen. Cotton Dutch white was 12 taels and 5 fen, medium sand white was 10 taels and 9 qian, and high goods were 11 taels. Transactions were scattered, and the market was stable. Tate & Lyle sugar was in greater demand, and the market stock was not large. Although there will be continued arrivals, the amount will not be large. Therefore, the market is more brisk, and the upper end is even more so. B-mark was 12 taels, 3 qian to 2.5 fen, and there was a shortage of goods. HX mark was 12 taels and 1 qian, HM mark was 11 taels and 7.5 qian, KY mark was 11 taels and 2 qian, and H mark was 11 taels and 9 qian. The market was stable and brisk.
