Heartbreaking Words 193

— Du Juan

Dear compatriots, for the past twenty days, the work of boycotting Japanese goods has indeed been very enthusiastic. There have been speeches, purchases, meetings, inspections, and the posting of slogans, all of which have been widespread throughout Shanghai. As a result, whether it is men and women in red or green, or old and young, everyone knows that Japanese goods should be boycotted, and everyone is unwilling to buy Japanese goods anymore. However, China is a vast country with abundant resources. Doing this kind of propaganda work in the metropolis is not enough. Everyone should devote some energy to going to the interior and the countryside to vigorously promote the boycott. Because transportation is less convenient in the interior and the countryside, and the people are less enlightened, they may not even know much about the invasion of the three northeastern provinces by the violent Japanese. And they are still buying and selling Japanese goods. Therefore, we must quickly go there to promote the boycott. Comrades, go to the interior, go to the countryside.

Random Notes from the Grass-Removing Studio

The Pole on the Barber's Load 194

When the Qing troops entered the customs, the people of the Ming Dynasty loved their hair more than their country. When the country was lost, their hair was inevitably shaved off. Two hundred and eighty-six years ago, Dodo went south of the Yangtze River. In April, he broke Yangzhou, and in May, Nanjing fell. He issued an order to shave hair, calling the barbers to walk on the streets with their loads. When they met people with long hair, they would catch them and shave them forcibly. If anyone resisted, they would cut off their heads and hang them on the pole of the load to show the public. Why did the barber's load have a pole later? This pole was originally prepared to hang people's heads. At that time, the Tartars and traitors also had words similar to modern slogans on the announcements. The two most cruel sentences were "Keep your head, but not your hair; keep your hair, but not your head." Those old people who loved their hair more than their country now love their hair more than their heads. Tens of thousands of people rose up everywhere to protect their hair and resist the Qing. Although these old people were somewhat confused about the importance of things in the past, they were relatively more ambitious than those who shaved immediately when they saw the knife and offered no resistance. It's a pity that they had no training and no good weapons on weekdays, so they were annihilated one after another in less than ten and a half months. If they had used the power to protect their hair to protect their country earlier, why would their descendants have been enslaved for 268 years? If we don't want to repeat their mistakes, we must (1) love the country more than our own family; (2) unite as soon as possible, learn real martial arts, and desperately resist foreign insults. Now most of the people across the country have understood this great truth, and they will surely rise up together to save the country. But there are still many muddleheaded people who live in a drunken dream. Well, if you want to know what it's like to lose your country, just think of the pole on the barber's load.

A Page from Dr. Sun Yat-sen's Imprisonment in London 195

— Zizai

After the failure of the first revolution in Guangzhou in 1895, Sun Yat-sen took refuge in Yokohama. Soon after, he traveled to Honolulu, and then went to the United States to promote the revolution. He was warmly welcomed by the overseas Chinese. Gradually, the Qing Legation in the United States detected him, and his actions became inconvenient. Therefore, he decided to go to London, the capital of England.

After arriving in London, he changed his name to Chen Wen, courtesy name Zai Zhi, and lived in the Krelitz Hotel. He learned that his teachers, Drs. Cantlie and Manson, had returned to England long ago. He scheduled a meeting with them, and the teachers and students were very happy. Cantlie's residence was very close to the Chinese Legation. He passed by the Legation almost every day on his way to Cantlie's residence. As a result, he met Deng Tingkeng, an interpreter at the Legation, on the way and had a conversation with him. After a while, Sun took out a gold watch to check the time. Deng asked to see it. The English phonetic spelling of the surname Sun was engraved on it. Deng suddenly realized and silently reported to Gong Xinzhan (Gong was the nephew of Minister Gong Zhaoyuan) to report to the Minister. Then he conspired with the British consultant, Macartney, to lure Mr. Sun into the three-story building of the Legation. He ordered Chinese and Western servants to guard him strictly in preparation for

Guangzhou, in order to claim credit and receive awards. The time was October 11th. Mr. Sun was trapped for six days. He repeatedly tried to get the English servants in the Legation to pass letters to Drs. Cantlie and Manson for help. They were all searched. The guards became even stricter. Mr. Sun was helpless and took prayer to God as a way to comfort himself. (Sun wrote to Elder Qu Fenghui of Hong Kong, describing the prayer in detail. In recent years, Christians have often used this letter to prove that Sun was a devout Christian.)

Alas, a mirror cannot be clear if it is not polished, and iron cannot be refined if it is not smelted. Heaven never cuts off all hope for people, especially for the savior of the Chinese nation. One day, Mr. Sun was chatting with an English servant, and the conversation involved Christianity. In a desperate situation, a plan was born. He asked about the Turkish emperor's massacre of Armenian Christians. Cole nodded. Sun then claimed to be a Christian believer who was hated by the Chinese Manchu emperor, who was jealous of the church. He had long wanted to capture and kill him, just like the Turkish emperor treated the Armenians. Now he was imprisoned in the Legation and would be sent back to the country within days and subjected to extreme punishment. Because the British government has always attached importance to humanity and protected believers, they acted secretly. If they could speak out righteously, not only would they be blessed by the Lord, but it would be a blessing for China and an honor for Britain. The words were earnest and sincere, and Mr. Cole was moved. Then he threw the secret letter into the coal basket and sent it to Drs. Cantlie and Manson.

Cantlie and others were shocked when they received the letter. They visited the superintendent of the Scotland Yard and officials from the Foreign Office, and sent a letter to the Earth newspaper to publish the whole story. The police station did not believe it at first. They hired a private detective to secretly investigate the actions of the Legation. As a result, British Prime Minister Salisbury had a major negotiation with the Chinese Legation. The citizens of London were particularly agitated. Minister Gong Zhaoyuan knew that the public's anger was difficult to offend, so he restored Mr. Sun's freedom on October 23rd. He was imprisoned for twelve days. When he left the Legation, there were crowds of people, all wanting to see the demeanor of the leader of the Chinese Revolutionary Party. Various newspapers competed to record the event. After escaping from danger, Mr. Sun traveled to Germany, France, Belgium and other countries to study politics for several months before returning to Japan. He also wrote a book called "Kidnapped in London" to be published.

The most ridiculous thing is that Gong Xinzhan was the one who planned Mr. Sun's imprisonment in the British Legation. When Mr. Sun died in Beiping in 1925, Gong was the Minister of the Interior and represented Duan Qirui in the Hall of the Altar of Land and Grain in the park. He bowed three times to the corpse of Mr. Sun. Gong was wondering what he felt when he recalled the past.

Northwest National Defense and Yang Hucheng 196

— Liang

The border provinces of our country are vast and sparsely populated, and the treasures are extremely rich. They have long been coveted by powerful neighbors. Since the Northeast Incident, the neglect of national defense has been fully exposed. Although the people of the country can cooperate and work together to plan the recovery of lost land, the essence has been destroyed. The recovery of vitality, but I do not know how much time it will take. It is particularly painful to say. Only the past is over. It is not too late to mend the fold after the sheep is lost. Since the Northeast has suffered a great robbery, the Northwest border area should be properly planned for a solid national defense as soon as possible. It is hoped that Red Russia will learn from the Japanese's old tricks of plotting the Northeast and destroy our fence. This is really the most important plan of today. The treasures covered in the northwest provinces are as rich as those in the northeast. It is only because of the obstruction of transportation that they have not been developed. This is due to the fact that the past officials in the northwest failed to do it on the ground. After Yang Hucheng took charge of the government in Shaanxi Province, all industries were thriving. Not only was the banditry eliminated, but the annual income was also extremely abundant. Compared with the desolate and chaotic situation when Feng Yuxiang's troops were stationed in Shaanxi a year ago, the difference cannot be measured by reason. Since Yang also served as the director of the Tongguan Camp, he regarded the consolidation of national defense and the development of the northwest as his responsibilities, and urged them to be realized as soon as possible. Yang has served in the northwest for decades, and he is highly respected. The governors of Gansu, Qinghai, Ningxia, and Xinjiang provinces have all expressed extreme obedience. The central government has also deeply trusted him, and he will be able to lead the group to achieve this goal. Even in the past, the people who changed in Gansu could wait for Yang to deal with it. It can be seen that Yang is one of the most popular people. The reporter deeply hopes that the people of the country will quickly shift their attention to the northwest and provide more assistance to the various industries in the northwest. Assisting Yang to complete this task is really the gospel of our country. If we are still indifferent and do not seek self-help, then the lessons of the Northeast are not far away, and national affairs will be even more unbearable.

The Current Situation of Qingyang, Suzhou 197

— Bing Ding

The Japanese are invading our country. The Treaty of Shimonoseki, which was lost to the Japanese, required the opening of concessions and commercial ports, which were mostly inland areas. For example, the opening of commercial ports in Jinan and the concessions in Suzhou can be seen here. If there is any negotiation, the treaty of the concession can be used to directly enter the inland. The Suzhou Japanese Concession is outside Panmen, in a place called Qingyangdi. When the Japanese leased the land, it also caused a sensation among the people of Suzhou. Before the late Qing Dynasty banned opium, Qingyangdi was within the sphere of influence of the Japanese. In accordance with the purpose of harming me with poison, opium dens were established everywhere and could be seen everywhere. The city signs of Qing paste and Guangshi were full of hope. In addition to opium dens, gambling dens were mixed in. Suzhou people have always been comfortable, and their lives are very prosperous. It has suddenly become a prosperous area. Speculators have set up theaters and restaurants. For a time, tourists regarded Qingyangdi as the destination. This was the heyday. Later, when the Huning Road was built, the Japanese once disputed, wanting to set up the station outside Panmen in Qingyang.

Be the First Patriotic Mother (Part 1) 198

— Hu Yanhong

Dear Mother:

I reluctantly suppressed my supreme sorrow and deepest enthusiasm and wrote you this letter of farewell. Now, nothing can stop my determination to join the army, I am willing to think of nothing, I only want to serve the country, and I am willing to die on the battlefield and be a loyal ghost of China. I can't take care of you, dear mother!

Don't be sad, don't be timid, you should be proud, because it is your dear son who is willing to be a martyr for the country, I have seen many mothers in other countries who also love their sons, but when the country is in trouble, they forget their private feelings and encourage each of their sons to go to work for their motherland, I hope you, dear mother, will be the first mother in China who loves her country more than her son. To be honest, it is sad to have a young man die on a cruel battlefield with bullets and bullets; however, if China is unfortunately destroyed, it is thousands of times more sad than dying in battle to have countless young people suffer bullying and abuse from foreigners, then you will not be able to love your son, watching your own flesh and blood writhing and moaning under the iron hooves of others.

Dear mother, be brave, wipe away the tears of love. With a solemn face, I warned your son: "Go ahead, son! I raised you for the country. If the country is in trouble, if you are not brave enough to go forward, you will fail me and insult me!

"

Dear mother, how I wish all mothers in China now would say this to their sons: "Goodbye, give my love to you, and I don't want to come back alive to see you!"

Next to it, so that the city will not decline. However, at that time, the people of Suzhou, in view of the advantages and disadvantages, fought hard to set it up outside Loumen. Due to traffic relations, Jinzhang emerged at the right time, and Qingyangdi gradually declined. The ban on gambling and opium was frequently issued. Opium dens and gambling dens gradually closed down. Theaters also moved to Jinzhang. The city of Qingyangdi fell sharply. The prosperity of the past is not what it used to be. Only a few secret opium dens are left. However, those who arrived thought that the place was desolate, and the Japanese had not invested in it. It was far less prosperous than Jinzhang. They were unwilling to go there. Until today, only uneven roads and empty, uninhabited wastelands can be seen. The Japanese consulate stands alone. From this, it can be seen that the cunning of the Japanese is not as good as that of the European and American countries, which can invest heavily to revitalize the market. The Japanese only have deceptive tricks to make the people of Suzhou foolish and think that they can be sheltered under them. They do not hesitate to spend huge sums of money to revitalize it. Once the adultery is exposed, like the collapse of an iceberg, it will become the Qingyangdi of today. Recently, the violent Japanese invaded and plundered our northeast. The Japanese living in Qingyangdi were disturbed by themselves and held residents' meetings one after another. First, the Japanese Consul went to the Public Security Bureau to discuss with Director Zou Jing the method of protecting overseas Chinese. They intended to take advantage of this period to ask soldiers to invade our inland. However, Zou replied that he could take full responsibility and ordered the police in the district to work hard to protect them. The people of Suzhou were also very peaceful and knew the cunning of the Japanese. They did not argue with them and advised each other not to enter Qingyangdi again. Even a rickshaw driver would not stay in Qingyangdi. The residents also moved away one after another. Therefore, the Qingyangdi area has been like a ghost domain for several days and is deserted.

An Art Exhibition Demonstrating National Spirit 199

— Qiang

When the famous painter Wang Jiyuan traveled in Europe, he witnessed the propaganda of the Japanese Art Association internationally. He had long had the ambition to dominate East Asia. He made Europeans and Americans know only Japan when it came to modern oriental culture, but not China. It was the most infuriating thing. He once held a solo exhibition in Paris, raising the status of the international art world. This time, after Mr. Wang returned to China, he contributed his firm will when the country was in trouble and held a European art exhibition in Shanghai, which is concerned by all countries, to show that the new Chinese national spirit is immortal. Since it was displayed in the Mingfu Library on October 1, Europeans, Americans, and Japanese have paid attention to it. No less than dozens of people have come to visit the meeting. Many young students in our country have come here. It is commendable to work hard to study academics in the midst of anti-Japanese voices. The most brilliant works of Mr. Wang are "Struggle" and "The God of Victory". The calmness of the color and the magnificence of the brushstrokes are still secondary. The performance of national spirit and the unique style of the East is thorough. Reading it can be encouraging. It is said that there will be an exhibition in the central location of the concession in a few days. (Move the reward to help the disaster)

Rotary Club of Storytelling

The Pestle of Knocking on Dreams (10) 200

— Cheng Zhanlu

According to the common practice in the imperial examination arena, any new scholars of the current session who have not yet obtained the qualifications for the imperial examination must be examined and recommended as undiscovered talents by the academy yamen before they are allowed to enter the arena to observe. At this time, the Supervising Education Commissioner had strict restrictions on newly advanced young people. Tao Chi was late for the examination three times and was not recorded into the register. Without this examination and selection, even if one possessed aspirations that were second to none and was rich in articles of high-mindedness and spirit, there would be no way to enter this provincial examination hall, which sought talent for the country. To reject him outside the arena, wouldn't it delay his three years of striving? He had undergone the baptism of the imperial examination. Not entering the provincial examination hall was more painful than being sentenced to death. He had no choice but to desperately cry out and run around.

He had run to all the important government offices in the provincial capital! He had cried out to all of them! He held his petition in vain, requesting the official authorities to transfer him into the arena. However, he was eventually shouted back by the gatekeeper's family member, whose belly was seen before their feet even left the door!

Tao Chi, whose fever for fame had reached the boiling point, still stood foolishly by the roadside, holding his petition. Whenever he encountered officials passing by with attendants, regardless of whether they were civil officials, military officials, river management officials, or salt affairs officials, he would always block the sedan chair and shout, delivering the petition requesting to be recommended into the arena. As a result, he was always rejected with the reply that "this official is not in charge of recording undiscovered talents," and the original petition was thrown back! The sedan chair carriers would then shout and leave.

Tao Chi, whose fever for fame had reached the boiling point, was almost going mad! Suddenly, he heard the sound of gongs and drums, mixed with shouts prohibiting pedestrians. The ceremonial guard was extremely grand! After the banners passed, there was a large sedan chair with green felt curtains on all sides. He knew that the examination hall was about to be sealed. He had to launch a final struggle, desperately blocking the sedan chair and shouting for help!

Inside the sedan chair with embroidered curtains, sat not a high-ranking official, but the family member of an official - the unmarried daughter of the Shandong Provincial Military Commander Tang. The accompanying military officers drew their swords, trying to frighten this reckless youth. However, Tao Chi, having resolved to be a wronged ghost under the sword rather than an examinee outside the arena, was not deterred by the drawn swords. He simply leaned on the ground and shouted for help.

Social News

Movie Sketch by Lu Mengshu 201

''Seed''

"Seed" is adapted from a novel. I haven't read the novel, but according to Miss Gladys Lehman, the screenwriter, in the "Press Sheet," the play and the original text differ quite a bit. However, the movie is definitely worth watching, as everyone must admit. I saw it a few months ago and was very satisfied.

The plot doesn't have bizarre twists and turns, or magnificent splendor. But the storytelling is subtle, meaningful, elegant and refreshing. That alone is enough for you to have a "daydream".

I very much agree with my friend Mu Luocha's statement that "in one or two years, ordinary facts are presented through artistic means." "Seed" is an artistic work that takes an ordinary story and expresses it through artistic means.

There are no peculiar plots, no grand sets, and no magnificent performances, but it is powerful enough to strike people's hearts.

A few years ago, we watched "Sunrise" and praised it endlessly. But "Sunrise" didn't have any peculiar plots, grand sets, or magnificent performances. It just told an ordinary story about ordinary life. What's so special about a banal story of a couple of adulterers? But when expressed through artistic means, you praise it endlessly. "Seed" is like that. Ten years of yearning, abandoning one's wife and children, is just a segment of an ordinary story in ordinary life. But when expressed through artistic means, it gives you great satisfaction. Only true art can give people a wonderful "fantasy" in film. Those incomplete, superficially magnificent things only make people feel like they are chewing wax.

"Seed" is a manifestation of true art. Its plot is very poignant, very elegant, and very handsome. Its story is very subtle, very fresh, and very graceful. The whole play gives people the feeling of listening to Cantonese folk songs, or listening to a violin solo in the city, or listening to the pipa of a merchant woman on the river under the moon. And yet

Page 22

It is warm and touching, poignant and appropriate, and yet it makes people unable to forget the characters in the play.

My friend Mu Luocha recently wrote a short story called "The Ditch," published in the fifth issue of "The Vanguard Monthly." That "Ditch" writes about the daily lives of men and women. The word "ditch," when pronounced by Cantonese people, has a very subtle interpretation in terms of pronunciation. I don't know if my friend was writing about the daily lives of men and women for the sake of this subtle interpretation when he took this word as the title, because we haven't seen each other in a long time. But "Seed" is completely about the "ditch." In fact, our desperate struggles under near civilization are indeed for the sake of the "ditch." If you know the "ditch," then you know the greatness of "Seed."

The theme of "Seed" is women resisting women, for the sake of "love." However, love, to put it bluntly, is just a "mask" for the "ditch." If you claim to have been baptized in the artistic culture of the city, you should admit what I'm saying.

In terms of the title, the focus is completely on "children." Indeed, the characters in the play already have five children. His wife resists women, on the surface, for the sake of those five children. However, in reality, it is for the sake of the "ditch."

Ah, the daily lives of men and women!

Precisely because it is the daily lives of men and women, it stirs up many sparkling waves and blows out many beautiful bubbles in the vast sea of people in everyday life. Just like "Seed" is a particularly sparkling wave in these many sparkling waves, a particularly beautiful shadow in these many beautiful bubbles. If you take it to symbolize scenery, it is like a burst of water flowers on a mirror-like blue wave under the afterglow of the setting sun. If you say it is a fantasy, then perhaps you had a particularly warm "daydream" in a love triangle in the film.

The original work of "Seed" is a very popular novel in the United States, with sales of hundreds of thousands and has been reprinted several times. The author, Charles G. Norris, has become known as a modern writer in the United States because of the popularity of this novel. As for the film, it is produced by Universal Company and has been translated into Chinese and called "The Faithless Man."

— Luther

Advance, advance, advance,

My dear people,

Listen! The iron horses clang,

Look! Flesh and blood soar,

The turbulent demons and monsters,

The ferocious beastly Japanese,

Have seized our Eastern Provinces,

Thousands of miles of land are sinking,

○○○

Advance, advance, advance,

My dear people,

Beat our war drums,

Raise our banners,

Light our torches,

Advance against the enemies,

Although we are weak and alone,

We have countless backings,

○○○

Advance, advance, advance,

My dear people,

Red blood boils in our chests,

Hot tears blur our eyes,

We raise a righteous army,

Cut open a bloody path,

Return our beautiful and splendid city,

○○○

Advance, advance, advance,

My dear people,

All the justice in the world,

Is only that might makes right,

The weak beg for mercy from others,

And people only mock and bully them,

We rely on a chest full of hot blood,

To dye red this general people's heart.

Advance, advance, advance,

Shorten our suffering,

Only charge, advance,

○○○

My dear people,

Everyone unite,

Farmers, workers, merchants, students, soldiers,

If you don't act at that time,

The enemy will come again to fortunately cut and trample,

Belgium's past glory,

If not resist, how can survive,

Advance, advance, advance,
